	eventsequence "cube_floor_P01"
	{
		particleType		= PT_3D_PLANE
		Emitrate			= 1
		Lifetime			= 2
		NumParticles		= 1
		TriggerTime			= 1000000000
		Layer				= 14
		BillBoardType		= BT_NONE
		SourceBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_SRCALPHA
		DestBlendMode	= D3DBLEND_DESTALPHA
		Trace				= TRUE

		Initial						Texture = "cube_light_P04.dds"
		Initial						Color = RGBA(1, 1, 1, 0)
		Fade so From 0.050 to 0.200	Color = RGBA(1, 1, 1, 0.800)
		Fade so From 0.300 to 0.600	Color = RGBA(1, 1, 1, 0)
		Initial						Size = XYZ(100, 30, 1)
		Fade so From 0.010 to 0.700	Size = XYZ(700, 30, 1)
		Initial						Rotate = XYZ(90, -45, 0)
		Initial						Velocity = XYZ(800, 8, 800)
		Fade so From 0.400 to 0.700	Velocity = XYZ(500, 8, 500)
	}
